Chinese Experts Establish New-Style Machine Factory 114

Small, Genuine Diesel Engines Appear: Most of the machines used in China are imported, and with the high price of gold, the leakage is increasing. It is urgent to reverse this situation. Now, many machine experts have set up factories to manufacture them themselves in order to meet the needs of the times. The factory is named the Shanghai Machine Factory and is building factory buildings and installing new German-style machine tools on Danyang Road in Yangshupu. They will first manufacture four-horsepower diesel engine water pumps, rice milling machines, flour mills, etc. Because of the high price and large horsepower of foreign goods, it is difficult for ordinary people to use them, and most of the domestic-made machines with less than eight horsepower are kerosene engines. Now that kerosene prices have soared to four times the price of diesel, it is extremely uneconomical. Therefore, a small engine is specially made that uses genuine diesel as fuel and is not imitated from foreign goods, but a product of many years of research and ingenuity. The machine body is strong, easy to move, and has sufficient horsepower, equivalent to the work of more than twenty people. The cost is reduced, requiring only five or six cents a day. The efficiency is equal to that of foreign goods, and the price is lower than that of any other country. The founders and staff of the factory are all engineering experts who have studied in Europe for many years and have served in the domestic industry for a long time. They are determined to adopt a rational management method to achieve the purpose of high-quality goods, low prices, and small profits but quick turnover. Many types of goods have already been released for people to choose from, and the opening day will be chosen soon.

Mr. Robert Dollar Arrives in Shanghai Today 115

Mr. Robert Dollar, the owner of the Dollar Steamship Line, is coming from the eastern United States to investigate the business conditions of the Dollar Steamship Line in various parts of the Far East. This is his thirty-sixth visit. He and his wife and secretary first arrived in Japan on the President Jefferson.

Recent Photo of Robert Dollar 116

After staying for a few days, they recently transferred to the President Grant in Kobe and are scheduled to arrive in Shanghai this morning. They will stay at Dollar Villa on Bixun Road for about a week, then go to Hong Kong and Luzon, and return to the United States via Europe. It is reported that the American Chamber of Commerce in Shanghai will host a banquet to welcome him.

Baoming Electric Company Feeds Electricity to Zhabei Water and Electricity Company 117

Public Utility Bureau Unifies Power Plants

First Step of the Plan Completed

The Municipal Public Utility Bureau, in order to achieve economic power generation, has stipulated a plan to unify the city's power plants. The first step is to urge small power plants to stop generating electricity and purchase electricity from large power plants for resale. This has been actively carried out in recent years. Various electrical companies are also well aware of the benefits, so they are happy to comply. For example, the Zhenru and Xianghua Electric Companies have already implemented feeding electricity to the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company one after another. The Pudong Electric Company has also signed a feeding electricity contract with the Huashang Electric Company and will soon stop generating electricity. The scale of the Baoming Electric Company is small, with only two violet oil generators with a total capacity of only about 230 kilowatts. Recently, the demand for electricity has gradually increased, and the maximum load is already above 200 kilowatts. Therefore, it is necessary to expand the equipment. The Public Utility Bureau believes that it is not as economical for small power plants to generate their own electricity as it is to purchase electricity from large power plants for resale, and the new Zhabei Jiansong Bridge Power Plant is about to generate electricity and is very close to Baoming Company, making it extremely convenient to connect the lines and power. Therefore, it instructed the company to stop expanding and negotiate with the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company to feed electricity. Subsequently, the two companies drafted a feeding electricity contract and submitted it to the Bureau for review. After correcting any inappropriate points, it was formally signed on September 15th and approved by the Bureau for record. It is learned that this contract will be implemented from January 1931. The first step of the plan for the two Public Utility Bureaus to unify the power plants has now been completed.

Fine of 15 Yuan for Printing Obsolete Calendars 118

Tang Yunji Bookstore in Siwen Lane on Datong Road, Huachang Printing Shop on North Chengdu Road, and Pei Zhang Bookstore on South Chengdu Road were all found by Inspector Ge Jingxuan of the Municipal Public Security Bureau to have printed obsolete calendars and almanacs, which violated the prohibition order. He reported this to the Special District Court, which issued a search warrant to the Xin Zha Police Station to send detectives. The three bookstores were found to have a large number of obsolete calendar books, which were sent to the Special Court. A summons was issued, but the owners of the bookstores did not arrive, so the court ordered that the hearing be rescheduled. This has been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, the police sent the bookstore owners Tang A gen, Hua Wenbin, and Wang Shaoshan to the Violation of Regulations Court. After questioning by Judge Shen Shumu, Tang, Hua, and Wang were each fined 15 yuan and the books were confiscated.
